PROVINCIAL   COUNCILS   ELECTIONS  ACT, No. 2 OF 1988
IN the exercise of the powers vested in me by section 7 (1) of the Provincial Councils Elections Act, No. 2 of 1988, I, Mahinda
Deshapriya, Commissioner of Elections do hereby appoint the Assistnat Returning Officers mentioned in Column II of the
Schedule hereto to assist the Returning Officer of the Administrative District specified in the corresponding entry in column
I of the above Schedule.
M
AHINDA D ESHAPRIY A,
Commissioner of Elections.
Elections Secretariat,
Rajagiriya.
16th September, 2013.
